          ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              <Separator />

              {/* 客户提交资料 */}
              <div>
                <h3 className="font-semibold text-sm mb-3 text-[#1E3A5F]">客户提交资料</h3>
                <div className="overflow-x-auto">
                  <table className="w-full text-sm">
                    <thead>
                      <tr className="border-b border-border">
                        <th className="text-left py-2 pr-4 text-muted-foreground font-normal whitespace-nowrap">序号</th>
                        <th className="text-left py-2 pr-4 text-muted-foreground font-normal whitespace-nowrap">资料类型</th>
                        <th className="text-left py-2 pr-4 text-muted-foreground font-normal whitespace-nowrap">内容摘要</th>
                        <th className="text-left py-2 text-muted-foreground font-normal whitespace-nowrap">提交时间</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      {subjectInfo?.background && (
                        <tr className="border-b border-border/50">
                          <td className="py-2 pr-4 whitespace-nowrap">1</td>
                          <td className="py-2 pr-4 whitespace-nowrap">文字陈述</td>
                          <td className="py-2 pr-4 text-muted-foreground max-w-xs truncate">{subjectInfo.background.slice(0, 60)}{subjectInfo.background.length > 60 ? '…' : ''}</td>
                          <td className="py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-muted-foreground">{new Date(report.created_at).toLocaleString('zh-CN')}</td>
                        </tr>
                      )}
                      {subjectInfo?.assets && (
                        <tr className="border-b border-border/50">
                          <td className="py-2 pr-4 whitespace-nowrap">2</td>
                          <td className="py-2 pr-4 whitespace-nowrap">资产/财务</td>
                          <td className="py-2 pr-4 text-muted-foreground max-w-xs truncate">{subjectInfo.assets.slice(0, 60)}{subjectInfo.assets.length > 60 ? '…' : ''}</td>
                          <td className="py-2 whitespace-nowrap text-muted-foreground">{new Date(report.created_at).toLocaleString('zh-CN')}</td>
                        </tr>
                      )}
                      {!subjectInfo?.background && !subjectInfo?.assets && (
                        <tr>
                          <td colSpan={4} className="py-3 text-muted-foreground text-center">暂无客户提交资料记录</td>
                        </tr>
                      )}
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                </div>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
            {/* 页脚 */}
            <div className="bg-[#1E3A5F]/5 border-t border-border px-6 py-2 flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-muted-foreground rounded-b-lg">
              <span>跨境家和·魔镜</span>
              <span>{report.report_number}</span>
              <span className="font-bold text-destructive">保密</span>
            </div>
          </Card>

          {/* ── 第3页：综合评估 + 魔镜建议 ── */}
          <Card className="mb-6">
            <CardHeader className="bg-[#1E3A5F]/5 rounded-t-lg pb-3">
              <CardTitle className="text-base text-[#1E3A5F]">第三页 · 综合评估 + 魔镜建议</CardTitle>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="space-y-5 pt-4">
              {/* 综合评级 */}
              <div className="border border-border rounded-lg p-4">
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-2">综合评级</p>
                <p className="text-xl font-bold" style={{ color: '#1E3A5F' }}>{String(data.overallRating) || '—'}</p>
                <div className="mt-3 grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-2 text-xs">
                  {[
                    { label: '🔴 红灯 - 高风险', desc: '发现重大风险信号' },
                    { label: '🟡 黄灯 - 需关注', desc: '存在部分风险信号' },
                    { label: '🟢 绿灯 - 低风险', desc: '未发现明显风险' },
                    { label: '⚪ 白灯 - 信息不足', desc: '公开信息有限' },
                  ].map((item) => (
                    <div key={item.label} className="bg-muted/40 rounded p-2">
                      <p className="font-medium">{item.label}</p>
                      <p className="text-muted-foreground">{item.desc}</p>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* 魔镜建议 */}
              <div>
                <h3 className="font-semibold text-sm mb-3 text-[#1E3A5F]">魔镜建议</h3>
                {safeRecs.length === 0 ? (
                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">暂无建议，请尝试重新分析。</p>
                ) : (
                  <div className="space-y-2">
                    {safeRecs.map((rec, i) => (
                      <div key={i} className="flex gap-3 text-sm p-3 bg-muted/30 rounded-lg">
                        <span className="w-6 h-6 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-xs shrink-0 font-bold text-white" style={{ background: '#1E3A5F' }}>
                          {i + 1}
                        </span>
                        <p className="text-foreground leading-relaxed">{rec}</p>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </CardContent>
            <div className="bg-[#1E3A5F]/5 border-t border-border px-6 py-2 flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-muted-foreground rounded-b-lg">
              <span>跨境家和·魔镜</span>
              <span>{report.report_number}</span>
              <span className="font-bold text-destructive">保密</span>
            </div>
          </Card>

          {/* ── 第4页：核查清单 + 搜索范围 + 免责声明 ── */}
          <Card className="mb-6">
            <CardHeader className="bg-[#1E3A5F]/5 rounded-t-lg pb-3">
              <CardTitle className="text-base text-[#1E3A5F]">第四页 · 核查清单 + 搜索范围 + 免责声明</CardTitle>
            </CardHeader>
            <CardContent className="space-y-6 pt-4">
              {/* 三类行动清单 */}
              <div className="grid md:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                {[
                  { icon: '🔍', title: '线上可查清单', items: safeChecklist.online ?? [] },
                  { icon: '📋', title: '主动核实清单', items: safeChecklist.proactive ?? [] },
                  { icon: '🏢', title: '实地核查清单', items: safeChecklist.onsite ?? [] },
                ].map((section) => (
                  <div key={section.title} className="bg-muted/30 rounded-lg p-3">
                    <h3 className="font-semibold text-sm mb-2">{section.icon} {section.title}</h3>
                    <ul className="space-y-1">
                      {section.items.length === 0
                        ? <li className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">暂无</li>
                        : section.items.map((item, i) => (
                          <li key={i} className="text-xs text-muted-foreground flex gap-1.5">
                            <span style={{ color: '#D4AF37' }}>•</span>{item}
                          </li>
                        ))}
                    </ul>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>

              <Separator />

              {/* 19个平台搜索范围 */}
              <div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-3">
                  <Globe className="w-4 h-4 text-[#1E3A5F]" />
                  <h3 className="font-semibold text-sm text-[#1E3A5F]">已查询 19 个公开平台</h3>
                </div>
                <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                  {PLATFORMS.map((group) => (
                    <div key={group.group} className="text-xs">
                      <p className="font-medium mb-1">{group.group}</p>
                      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                        {group.items.map((item) => (
                          <span key={item} className="px-2 py-0.5 bg-muted rounded text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1">
                            ✓ {item}
                          </span>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              <Separator />

              {/* 免责声明 */}
              <div className="border border-border rounded-lg p-4 bg-muted/20">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                  <Shield className="w-4 h-4 text-[#1E3A5F]" />
                  <h3 className="font-semibold text-sm text-[#1E3A5F]">免责声明</h3>
                </div>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
                  本报告由跨境家和·魔镜 AI 系统根据用户提供信息及公开数据自动生成，仅供参考，不构成任何法律建议或法律意见。
                  魔镜 AI 不对报告的完整性、准确性及时效性作出任何保证。用户应自行判断报告内容的适用性，并承担相应风险。
                  本报告依据 PIPEDA（加拿大个人信息保护及电子文件法）及中国个人信息保护法相关规定处理数据，严格保密，禁止用于商业用途。
                  跨境家和为律师引荐平台，不直接提供法律服务，所有法律服务由持牌合作律师独立提供。
                </p>
                <p className="text-xs text-[#1E3A5F] font-medium mt-2">
                  © 2026 跨境家和 · www.crossborder-jiahe.com · 本报告属于保密文件
                </p>
              </div>
            </CardContent>
            <div className="bg-[#1E3A5F]/5 border-t border-border px-6 py-2 flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-muted-foreground rounded-b-lg">
              <span>跨境家和·魔镜</span>
              <span>{report.report_number}</span>
              <span className="font-bold text-destructive">保密</span>
            </div>
          </Card>

        {/* PDF内容区结束 */}
        </div>

        {/* 操作按钮（PDF 区外） */}
        <div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row gap-3 mt-6">
          <Button variant="outline" className="flex-1" onClick={handleExportPDF} disabled={exportingPDF}>
            {exportingPDF
              ? <><Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 mr-2 animate-spin" />生成PDF中…</>
              : <><Download className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />下载PDF报告</>}
          </Button>
          <Button
            className="flex-1 text-white hover:opacity-90"
            style={{ background: '#1E3A5F' }}
            onClick={handleUpdate}
            disabled={updating}
          >
            {updating
              ? <><Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 mr-2 animate-spin" />更新中…</>
              : <><Upload className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />补充新证据/材料</>}
          </Button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* ── 补充材料弹窗 ── */}
      <Dialog open={showUpdateDialog} onOpenChange={setShowUpdateDialog}>
        <DialogContent className="max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] md:max-w-lg">
          <DialogHeader>
            <DialogTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <PlusCircle className="w-5 h-5" style={{ color: '#D4AF37' }} />
              补充新证据 / 材料
            </DialogTitle>
            <DialogDescription>填写补充说明或上传文件后，魔镜将重新分析并更新报告。</DialogDescription>
          </DialogHeader>
          <div className="space-y-4 py-2">
            <div>
              <Label htmlFor="new-evidence" className="text-sm font-normal">补充说明（可选）</Label>
              <Textarea
                id="new-evidence"
                value={newEvidence}
                onChange={(e) => setNewEvidence(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="请描述新发现的情况、证据或需要重新评估的信息…"
                className="mt-1"
                rows={4}
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <Label className="text-sm font-normal">上传文件（可选，最多 5 个）</Label>
              <div className="mt-1 border-2 border-dashed border-border rounded-lg p-4 text-center hover:border-primary/50 transition-colors">
                <Upload className="w-8 h-8 mx-auto text-primary mb-2" />
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-2">支持 PDF、Word、图片，单文件最大 10MB</p>
                <input type="file" multiple id="update-file-upload" onChange={handleNewFileSelect} className="hidden" accept=".pdf,.doc,.docx,.jpg,.jpeg,.png" />
                <label htmlFor="update-file-upload" className="cursor-pointer">
                  <Button variant="default" size="sm" asChild>
                    <span className="flex items-center gap-2"><Upload className="w-4 h-4" />选择文件</span>
                  </Button>
                </label>
              </div>
              {newFiles.length > 0 && (
                <div className="mt-2 space-y-1">
                  {newFiles.map((f, i) => (
                    <div key={i} className="flex items-center gap-2 p-2 bg-secondary rounded text-sm">
                      <FileText className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
                      <span className="flex-1 truncate">{f.name}</span>
                      <button onClick={() => setNewFiles((prev) => prev.filter((_, idx) => idx !== i))} className="text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive">
                        <X className="w-4 h-4" />
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
          <DialogFooter className="flex-col sm:flex-row gap-2">
            <Button variant="outline" onClick={() => setShowUpdateDialog(false)} className="flex-1">取消</Button>
            <Button onClick={handleSubmitUpdate} disabled={updating} className="flex-1 text-white" style={{ background: '#1E3A5F' }}>
              <Upload className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />提交并重新分析
            </Button>
          </DialogFooter>
        </DialogContent>
      </Dialog>

      {/* 重新分析进度遮罩 */}
      {updating && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex items-center justify-center bg-background/70 backdrop-blur-sm">
          <div className="bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-6 text-center space-y-3 max-w-xs w-full mx-4 shadow-2xl">
            <Loader2 className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto animate-spin" style={{ color: '#D4AF37' }} />
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">正在根据补充材料重新分析…</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Groq · DeepSeek · Qwen 并行处理中</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

取响应最快的有效结果作为主体\n  const primary = valid.sort((a, b) => a.ms - b.ms)[0];\n  const base = primary.data as Record<string, unknown>;\n\n  // 合并其他模型的 riskSignals（去重 + 补充）\n  const allSignals: Array<{ allSignals.findIndex((x) => x.category?.toLowerCase() === key);\n        if (idx >= 0) {\n          const levels = [\'low\', \'medium\', \'high\'];\n          if (levels.indexOf(s.level) > levels.indexOf(allSignals[idx].level)) {\n            allSignals[idx].level = s.level;\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // 合并建议（去重）\n  const allRecs: string[] = [];\n  const seenRecs string[] = [];\n  if (valid.length > 1) {\n    for (const cat of seenCategories) {\n      const levels = valid.map((r) => {\n        const d = r.data as Record<string, unknown>;\n        const rawSignals = Array.isArray(d?.riskSignals) ? d.riskSignals : [];\n        const signals = (rawSignals as unknown[]).filter(\n          (s): s is { category: string; level: string } =>\n string[];\n\n      if (levels.includes(\'high\') && levels.includes(\'low\')) {\n        divergences.push(`「${cat}」风险等级存在分歧，建议进一步核实`);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  const modelCount = valid.length;\n  const synthNote = modelCount >= 2\n    ? `已综合 ${modelCount} 个 AI 模型分析${divergences.length > 0 ? \'，存在分歧点见下\' : \'，各模型结论高度一致\'}`\n    : \'由单一模型生成\';\n\n  return {\n    ...base,\n    riskSignals: allSignals,\n    recommendations: allRecs.slice(0, 5),\n    _meta: {\n      modelsUsed: modelCount,\n      totalModels: results.length,\n      fastestModel: primary.label,\n      fastestMs: primary.ms,\n      synthesisNote: synthNote,\n      divergences,\n    },\n  };\n}\n\n// ── 主处理器 ──────────────────────────────────────────────\nDeno.serve(async (req) => {\n  if (req.method === \'OPTIONS\') {\n    return new Response(null, { status: 204, headers: CORS });\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const body = await req.json();\n    const {\n      subjectName = \'\',\n      relationship = \'\',\n      background = \'\',\n      assets = \'\',\n      guestMode = false,\n    } = body;\n\n    if (!subjectName.trim()) {\n      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: \'请填写调查对象姓名\' }), {\n        status: 400,\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\', ...CORS },\n      });\n    }\n\n    // 非 guest 模式需验证 Auth\n    if (!guestMode) {\n      const authHeader = req.headers.get(\'Authorization\');\n      if (!authHeader) {\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: \'未登录\' }), {\n          status: 401,\n          headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\', ...CORS },\n        });\n      }\n      const supabase = createClient(supabaseUrl, supabaseServiceKey);\n      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser(authHeader.replace(\'Bearer \', \'\'));\n      if (!user) {\n        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: \'用户未登录\' }), {\n          status: 401,\n          headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\', ...CORS },\n        });\n      }\n    }\n\n    // 拼接全部输入文本用于语言检测\n    const fullText = [subjectName, relationship, background, assets].join(\' \');\n    const lang = detectLanguage(fullText);\n    const prompt = buildPrompt(subjectName, relationship, background, assets, lang);\n\n    console.log(`[magic_mirror] lang=${lang}, subject="${subjectName}"`);\n\n    // ── 按语言路由并行调用 ──────────────────────────────\n    const calls: Promise<{ label: string; data: Record<string, unknown> | null; ms: number }>[] = [];\n\n    // 英文或混合 → 加入 Groq\n    if (lang === \'en\' || lang === \'mixed\') {\n      if (GROQ_API_KEY) {\n        calls.push(callModel({\n          baseUrl: \'https://api.groq.com/openai/v1\',\n          apiKey: GROQ_API_KEY,\n          model: \'llama-3.3-70b-versatile\',\n          prompt,\n          label: \'Groq-Llama3.3-70B\',\n        }));\n      } else {\n        console.warn(\'[magic_mirror] GROQ_API_KEY not configured, skipping Groq\');\n      }\n    }\n\n    // 中文、英文、混合 → 硅基流动 Qwen2.5-7B\n    if (SILICONFLOW_API_KEY) {\n      calls.push(callModel({\n        baseUrl: \'https://api.siliconflow.cn/v1\',\n        apiKey: SILICONFLOW_API_KEY,\n        model: \'Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct\',\n        prompt,\n        label: \'SiliconFlow-Qwen2.5-7B\',\n      }));\n\n      // 中文、英文、混合 → 硅基流动 DeepSeek-V3\n      calls.push(callModel({\n        baseUrl: \'https://api.siliconflow.cn/v1\',\n        apiKey: SILICONFLOW_API_KEY,\n        model: \'deepseek-ai/DeepSeek-V3\',\n        prompt,\n        label: \'SiliconFlow-DeepSeek-V3\',\n      }));\n    } else {\n      console.warn(\'[magic_mirror] SILICONFLOW_API_KEY not configured, skipping SiliconFlow\');\n    }\n\n    if (calls.length === 0) {\n      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: \'AI 服务密钥未配置，请联系管理员\' }), {\n        status: 503,\n        headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\', ...CORS },\n      });\n    }\n\n    // 取最快成功的模型结果（Promise.any），超时 25s 兜底\n    const raceWithTimeout = <T,>(promises: Promise<T>[], ms: number): Promise<T> =>\n      Promise.any([\n        ...promises,\n        new Promise<T>((_, reject) => setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(\'timeout\')), ms)),\n      ]);\n\n    let reportData;\n    try {\n      // 先等最快的一路返回\n      const first = await raceWithTimeout(calls, 25000);\n      reportData = synthesize([first], subjectName);\n    } catch {\n      // 如果 Promise.any 全部失败，尝试 allSettled 取任何成功的结果\n      const settled = await Promise.allSettled(calls);\n      const successes = settled\n        .filter((r): r is PromiseFulfilledResult<Awaited<(typeof calls)[0]>> => r.status === \'fulfilled\')\n        .map((r) => r.value);\n      if (successes.length === 0) throw new Error(\'所有 AI 模型均无响应，请稍后重试\');\n      reportData = synthesize(successes, subjectName);\n    }\n\n    console.log(`[magic_mirror] synthesized, modelsUsed=${(reportData._meta as Record<string, unknown>)?.modelsUsed}`);\n\n    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ reportData, lang }), {\n      status: 200,\n      headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\', ...CORS },\n    });\n  } catch (err: unknown) {\n    const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);\n    console.error(\'[magic_mirror ERROR]\', msg);\n    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: msg || \'服务内部错误\' }), {\n      status: 500,\n      headers: { \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\', ...CORS },\n    });\n  }\n});\n'}]}

| 记录类型 | 主机记录 | 记录值 |
|---------|---------|--------|
| CNAME | `www` | 秒哒给你的 CNAME 地址（见第二步） |
| CNAME | `@` | 秒哒给你的 CNAME 地址（见第二步） |

---

### 第二步：在秒哒绑定自定义域名

在秒哒编辑器界面找「设置」或「发布」→「自定义域名」，输入 `crossborderjiahe.com` 后，秒哒会给你一个 **CNAME 目标地址**，把那个地址填到上面阿里云的记录值里。

---

## 关于「修改后能否继续更新」

**完全可以。** 绑定域名后，你在秒哒这里修改代码、点击发布，`crossborderjiahe.com` 自动更新，域名绑定是一次性配置。

---

中文：千人律所资深律师 / 中国执业律师（1998年起） / 美加理财顾问双执照 / 跨国投资专家 / 婚姻家事业务\n  - 英文：Senior Attorney at Thousand-Lawyer Firm / Licensed Attorney in China (since 1998) / Dual Licensed Financial Advisor in US & Canada / Cross-Border Investment Expert / Family Law Practice\n- 展示四段履历：\n  1. 中文：1998年，邱律取得中国律师执照，加入一家在中国市场综合排名前十、拥有逾千名执业律师、在国内30个城市设有办公室的大型律师事务所，长期深耕跨国投资与婚姻家事业务。\n     英文：In 1998, Attorney Alice Qiu obtained her Chinese lawyer license and joined a large law firm ranked in the top ten in the Chinese market, with over a thousand practicing lawyers and offices in 30 cities across the country. She has long been deeply involved in cross-border investment and family law practice.\n  2. 中文：2005年与家人定居加拿大后，邱律凭借对两国法律体系的深度理解，专门负责为国内同事来加拿大投资或处理婚姻家事争议，在各省采购专业律师服务。在这个过程中，她发现许多跨境家庭的离婚与继承纠纷，仅靠法律手段往往难以彻底解决——结合保险、保本基金等金融工具，才能更全面地帮助到客户。为此，她相继取得了美国与加拿大的理财顾问牌照。\n     英文：After settling in Canada with her family in 2005, Attorney Qiu, with her deep understanding of the legal systems of both countries, specialized in assisting domestic colleagues with investments in Canada or handling family law disputes, procuring professional legal services in various provinces. In this process, she discovered that many cross-border family divorce and inheritance disputes could not be completely resolved by legal means alone—combining insurance, principal-protected funds, and other financial tools could provide more comprehensive assistance to clients. For this reason, she successively obtained financial advisor licenses in the United States and Canada.\n  3. 中文：多年来，邱律亲眼目睹了无数本可避免的家庭悲剧：夫妻因大声争吵被追究刑事责任、母亲因帮孩子做作业失去监护权、老人因不了解加拿大法律向子女索要赡养费导致关系破裂……这些经历让她决心创立跨境家和，用教育与陪伴守护每一个跨境家庭。\n     英文：Over the years, Attorney Qiu has witnessed countless avoidable family tragedies: couples facing criminal charges for loud arguments, mothers losing custody for helping children with homework, elderly parents demanding alimony from their children due to unfamiliarity with Canadian law, leading to broken relationships... These experiences led her to establish CrossBorder JiaHe, using education and companionship to protect every cross-border family.\n  4. 中文：「无论是国王还是农夫，家庭和睦是最幸福的。」这句话是我创立跨境家和的初心。\n     英文：「Whether king or peasant, family harmony is the greatest happiness.」This quote is the original intention behind my founding of CrossBorder JiaHe.\n\n#### 3.3.3 引荐平台定位说明\n- 展示区块标题：\n  - 中文：连接您与持牌专业律师\n  - 英文：Connecting You with Licensed Professional Lawyers\n- 展示区块副标题：\n  - 中文：跨境家和是律师引荐平台，我们连接您与持牌专业律师。所有入驻律师均经过资质审核，我们不直接提供法律服务。\n  - 英文：CrossBorder JiaHe is a lawyer referral platform. 提示系统异常，请稍后重试 |\n| 用户输入信息不完整 | 提示必填项未填写 |\n| 紧急家庭安全问题 | 页面红色突出提示：如遇紧急家庭安全问题，请立即拨打 911 |\n| 浏览器不支持的语言 | 默认使用中文 |\n| 翻译文件加载失败 | 显示中文内容并提示用户刷新页面 |\n| AI小助手被问及法律判断 | 回复：我仅提供信息引导，不构成法律建议。个案咨询请通过平台预约持牌律师。 |\n| 移动端访问 | 导航栏自动折叠为汉堡菜单，页面自适应 |\n| 会员到期前7天 | 系统自动提醒用户续费或升级 |\n| 用户尝试升级会员 | 计算差价并引导支付 |\n\n---\n\n## 7. 验收标准\n\n1. 用户访问首页，浏览10个区块内容，了解跨境家和的品牌理念、三大核心服务与引荐平台信任体系\n2. 中文：千人律所资深律师 / 中国执业律师（1998年起） / 美加理财顾问双执照 / 跨国投资专家 / 婚姻家事业务\n  - 英文：Senior Attorney at Thousand-Lawyer Firm / Licensed Attorney in China (since 1998) / Dual Licensed Financial Advisor in US & Canada / Cross-Border Investment Expert / Family Law Practice\n- 展示四段履历：\n  1. 中文：1998年，邱律取得中国律师执照，加入一家在中国市场综合排名前十、拥有逾千名执业律师、在国内30个城市设有办公室的大型律师事务所，长期深耕跨国投资与婚姻家事业务。\n     英文：In 1998, Attorney Alice Qiu obtained her Chinese lawyer license and joined a large law firm ranked in the top ten in the Chinese market, with over a thousand practicing lawyers and offices in 30 cities across the country. She has long been deeply involved in cross-border investment and family law practice.\n  2. 中文：2005年与家人定居加拿大后，邱律凭借对两国法律体系的深度理解，专门负责为国内同事来加拿大投资或处理婚姻家事争议，在各省采购专业律师服务。在这个过程中，她发现许多跨境家庭的离婚与继承纠纷，仅靠法律手段往往难以彻底解决——结合保险、保本基金等金融工具，才能更全面地帮助到客户。为此，她相继取得了美国与加拿大的理财顾问牌照。\n     英文：After settling in Canada with her family in 2005, Attorney Qiu, with her deep understanding of the legal systems of both countries, specialized in assisting domestic colleagues with investments in Canada or handling family law disputes, procuring professional legal services in various provinces. In this process, she discovered that many cross-border family divorce and inheritance disputes could not be completely resolved by legal means alone—combining insurance, principal-protected funds, and other financial tools could provide more comprehensive assistance to clients. For this reason, she successively obtained financial advisor licenses in the United States and Canada.\n  3. 中文：多年来，邱律亲眼目睹了无数本可避免的家庭悲剧：夫妻因大声争吵被追究刑事责任、母亲因帮孩子做作业失去监护权、老人因不了解加拿大法律向子女索要赡养费导致关系破裂……这些经历让她决心创立跨境家和，用教育与陪伴守护每一个跨境家庭。\n     英文：Over the years, Attorney Qiu has witnessed countless avoidable family tragedies: couples facing criminal charges for loud arguments, mothers losing custody for helping children with homework, elderly parents demanding alimony from their children due to unfamiliarity with Canadian law, leading to broken relationships... These experiences led her to establish CrossBorder JiaHe, using education and companionship to protect every cross-border family.\n  4. 中文：「无论是国王还是农夫，家庭和睦是最幸福的。」这句话是我创立跨境家和的初心。\n     英文：「Whether king or peasant, family harmony is the greatest happiness.」This quote is the original intention behind my founding of CrossBorder JiaHe.\n\n#### 3.3.3 引荐平台定位说明\n- 展示区块标题：\n  - 中文：连接您与持牌专业律师\n  - 英文：Connecting You with Licensed Professional Lawyers\n- 展示区块副标题：\n  - 中文：跨境家和是律师引荐平台，我们连接您与持牌专业律师。所有入驻律师均经过资质审核，我们不直接提供法律服务。\n  - 英文：CrossBorder JiaHe is a lawyer referral platform. 提示系统异常，请稍后重试 |\n| 用户输入信息不完整 | 提示必填项未填写 |\n| 紧急家庭安全问题 | 页面红色突出提示：如遇紧急家庭安全问题，请立即拨打 911 |\n| 浏览器不支持的语言 | 默认使用中文 |\n| 翻译文件加载失败 | 显示中文内容并提示用户刷新页面 |\n| AI小助手被问及法律判断 | 回复：我仅提供信息引导，不构成法律建议。个案咨询请通过平台预约持牌律师。 |\n| 移动端访问 | 导航栏自动折叠为汉堡菜单，页面自适应 |\n| 会员到期前7天 | 系统自动提醒用户续费或升级 |\n| 用户尝试升级会员 | 计算差价并引导支付 |\n\n---\n\n## 7. 验收标准\n\n1. 用户访问首页，浏览10个区块内容，了解跨境家和的品牌理念、三大核心服务与引荐平台信任体系\n2. In this process, she discovered that many cross-border family divorce and inheritance disputes could not be completely resolved by legal means alone—combining insurance, principal-protected funds, and other financial tools could provide more comprehensive assistance to clients. For this reason, she successively obtained financial advisor licenses in the United States and Canada.\n  3. 中文：多年来，邱律亲眼目睹了无数本可避免的家庭悲剧：夫妻因大声争吵被追究刑事责任、母亲因帮孩子做作业失去监护权、老人因不了解加拿大法律向子女索要赡养费导致关系破裂……这些经历让她决心创立跨境家和，用教育与陪伴守护每一个跨境家庭。\n     英文：Over the years, Attorney Qiu has witnessed countless avoidable family tragedies: couples facing criminal charges for loud arguments, mothers losing custody for helping children with homework, elderly parents demanding alimony from their children due to unfamiliarity with Canadian law, leading to broken relationships... These experiences led her to establish CrossBorder JiaHe, using education and companionship to protect every cross-border family.\n  4. 中文：「无论是国王还是农夫，家庭和睦是最幸福的。」这句话是我创立跨境家和的初心。\n     英文：「Whether king or peasant, family harmony is the greatest happiness.」This quote is the original intention behind my founding of CrossBorder JiaHe.\n\n#### 3.3.3 引荐平台定位说明\n- 展示区块标题：\n  - 中文：连接您与持牌专业律师\n  - 英文：Connecting You with Licensed Professional Lawyers\n- 展示区块副标题：\n  - 中文：跨境家和是律师引荐平台，我们连接您与持牌专业律师。所有入驻律师均经过资质审核，我们不直接提供法律服务。\n  - 英文：CrossBorder JiaHe is a lawyer referral platform. For individual case consultations, please book a licensed lawyer through the platform.\n\n### 3.11 国际化功能\n\n#### 3.11.1 语言切换机制\n- 使用react-i18next实现国际化支持\n- 支持中文（zh）和英文（en）两种语言\n- 所有页面文本使用翻译键替换硬编码文本\n- 语言切换时保持当前页面路径不变，仅切换内容\n\n#### 3.11.2 默认语言规则\n- 默认语言跟随用户浏览器语言设置\n- 支持通过URL参数切换语言\n- 用户手动切换语言后，保存语言偏好\n\n#### 3.11.3 翻译文件\n- 翻译内容基于以下文件：\n  - 中文原文：/workspace/app-cc2fqeuowe81/tasks/website_content_for_translation.md\n  - 英文翻译：/workspace/app-cc2fqeuowe81/tasks/english_translation_v1.md\n- 品牌术语统一翻译对照：\n  - 跨境家和 → CrossBorder JiaHe\n  - 邱律 → Attorney Alice Qiu\n  - 蓝仙女 → Blue Fairy\n  - 家和小助手 → JiaHe Assistant\n  - 魔镜 → Magic Mirror\n  - 家和成长营 → JiaHe Growth Camp\n  - AI调解 → AI Mediation\n  - 家和协商室 → JiaHe Mediation Room\n  - 安心认证 → Peace of Mind Certification\n  - 德和衡 → DeHeng Law Firm\n  - 免费会员 → Free Member\n  - 普通会员 → Standard Member\n  - 高级会员 → Premium Member\n- 去除所有 i18n key 占位符，完成全部翻译\n\n---\n\n## 4. 业务规则与逻辑\n\n### 4.1 会员权益规则\n- 游客：注册后获得1次免费魔镜体验\n- 免费会员：2份免费魔镜报告 + 免费36分钟AI辅助中心\n- 普通会员：\n  - 价格：年付¥2,999 或 月付¥249\n  - 权益：10次/月魔镜报告 + ¥100/小时AI辅助中心 + 9折预约律师 + ¥399/次安心认证 + 线上+线下家和成长营\n- 高级会员：\n  - 价格：年付¥5,999 或 月付¥599\n  - 权益：20次/月魔镜报告 + ¥50/小时AI辅助中心 + 8折预约律师 + 免费1次安心认证 + 蓝标专属家和成长营\n- 超额使用：单次购买¥49/份初筛报告\n\n### 4.2 会员升级规则\n- 升级路径：游客 → 免费会员 → 普通会员 → 高级会员\n- 升级方式：支付差价即可升级\n- 到期提醒：到期前7天系统自动提醒用户续费或升级\n\n### 4.3 魔镜报告生成规则\n\n#### 4.3.1 PDF文件处理\n- 用户上传最多5个PDF文件\n- 系统提取PDF文本内容\n- AI分析关键信息（姓名、公司、地址、日期等）\n\n#### 4.3.2 多平台搜索\n- 系统自动搜索以下12个平台：\n  1. 百度搜索\n  2. Google搜索\n  3. 微博\n  4. 知乎\n  5. 微信公众号\n  6. 今日头条\n  7. 抖音/TikTok\n  8. B站\n  9. 小红书\n  10. 新闻媒体（新华/人民等）\n  11. GitHub（技术背景）\n  12. 用户上传PDF内容分析\n- 特殊平台处理：\n  - 天眼查/裁判文书网/LinkedIn：显示「已尝试查询/需人工核实」\n\n#### 4.3.3 实时搜索进度展示\n- 逐平台显示查询进度（类似终端日志效果）\n- 每个平台显示查询状态：\n  - 查询中（进度条动画）\n  - 已完成（显示找到的相关信息条数）\n  - 受限（显示「已尝试查询/需人工核实」）\n  - 失败（显示错误提示）\n\n#### 4.3.4 报告生成\n- 生成时间：3分钟内\n- 报告格式：固定4页PDF\n- 报告编号：会员姓名-被查人姓名-日期-序号\n\n#### 4.3.5 报告内容结构\n- 第1页：封面\n- 第2页：核验信息 + 风险发现 + 参考资料\n- 第3页：综合评估\n- 第4页：核查清单\n- 四色风险标签：红（高风险）/黄（注意）/绿（正常）/白（无数据）\n\n### 4.4 报告更新规则\n- 用户可在会员中心或报告详情页补充新证据/材料\n- 系统基于新证据重新生成报告\n- 保留原报告版本记录\n\n### 4.5 文件上传规则\n- 支持格式：PDF\n- 文件数量限制：最多5个\n- 文件大小限制：单个文件不超过10MB\n\n### 4.6 语言切换规则\n- 用户点击语言切换按钮时，页面内容立即切换为对应语言\n- 切换后保持当前页面路径和用户操作状态\n- 语言偏好保存在本地存储中\n- 首次访问时，根据浏览器语言设置自动选择语言\n\n### 4.7 AI小助手规则\n- AI小助手语言自动跟随页面语言\n- 首次使用时展示免责提示\n- AI助手仅提供信息引导，不做法律判断\n- 涉及具体法律问题时，引导用户预约持牌律师\n\n### 4.8 律师引荐规则\n- 所有入驻律师均经过资质审核\n- 用户信息全程匿名隐私保护\n- 已认证律师展示安心认证标识\n\n### 4.9 数据存储规则\n\n#### 4.9.1 reports表\n- 存储报告元数据：\n  - 报告ID\n  - 会员ID\n  - 被查人姓名\n  - 报告编号\n  - 生成日期\n  - 风险等级\n  - 状态（已完成/更新中）\n\n#### 4.9.2 search_results表\n- 存储各平台搜索结果：\n  - 搜索结果ID\n  - 报告ID\n  - 平台名称\n  - 查询状态（已完成/受限/失败）\n  - 找到的相关信息条数\n  - 搜索结果内容\n\n#### 4.9.3 uploaded_files表\n- 存储上传的PDF文件信息：\n  - 文件ID\n  - 报告ID\n  - 文件名称\n  - 文件大小\n  - 上传时间\n  - 文件路径\n\n---\n\n## 5. SkillObservation(content='Base directory for this skill: /workspace/app-cc2fqeuowe81/.skills/supabase-server\n\n# Supabase Backend\n\nApplies to all frontend stacks (Web / MiniProgram / App). Covers Supabase server-side Schema, RLS, Edge Functions, Storage, Realtime, and Auth configuration.\n\n## Initial Setup\n\n- Use `supabase_init` to initialize the database or start it from a paused state\n\n## Schema Design\n\n- Minimize tables and columns; merge functionalities into single tables when possible\n- Set database-level default values for required fields\n  - Example: `owner_id uuid not null default auth.uid()`\n  - Example: `order_number text UNIQUE NOT NULL` — use a trigger bound to insert logic to auto-generate the order number\n- For multi-table relations, define them clearly to avoid missing link fields\n- ENUM values require explicit casts\n- **NEVER interact with `supabase/migrations/` directory** (including ls, cat, view)\n- Always apply changes through incremental migrations\n- Verify database state by querying table structure using `supabase_execute_sql`\n- Try to combine tasks and execute all SQL in a single run\n- Always consider performance and speed optimization\n- Disallow SQL statements with silent or ambiguous success semantics (e.g., `IF NOT EXISTS`, `IF EXISTS`) — all operations must fail explicitly when schema or data deviates from expectations\n\n## Data Insertion\n\n**Must-Add:**\n- System-required data (e.g., categories, form dropdown options)\n- **For image URLs**: Use `image_search` to get real URLs — **NEVER** use placeholder URLs like `https://placeholder-image.jpg`\n- Add initial seed data (INSERT INTO) in the migration SQL, using `image_search` for real image URLs\n\n**Allowed:**\n- Homepage display data (e.g., showcases, course previews, products)\n- Demo data (e.g., sample exam sets)\n\n**Forbidden:**\n- User data\n- User activity history (e.g., lottery, orders)\n- Real personal names or any privacy-related info\n\n## SQL Modification\n\n- If you have full context in memory, prioritize using it directly\n- If unsure about current data structure, query it first; do not rely on migration files\n- Under no circumstances should you view or modify migration files\n- If frontend requires a feature without a corresponding table, policy, or edge function, you may add it afterward\n- When modifying business data (non-DDL, policy, RPC, etc.), use `supabase_execute_sql`\n- Before writing api.ts, read the corresponding `supabase/migrations/*.sql` to confirm NOT NULL constraints for every column — context compression may lose field details; migrations are the ground truth\n\n## Security Policies (RLS)\n\n### Design Principles\n\n- **Every table MUST have RLS enabled** — no exceptions, regardless of whether login auth exists\n- **Full coverage per table**: Explicitly define policies for every combination of SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE × {anon, authenticated, admin}. **Never leave any blank** — missing policies silently return empty data or 0 affected rows\n  - Per-table review checklist: anon × {S/I/U/D}, authenticated × {S/I/U/D}, admin × {S/I/U/D}\n  - Anticipate future features: add corresponding constraints now for role×operation combinations that may be needed later\n- **INSERT always requires a matching SELECT**: Any role granted INSERT permission MUST also have a SELECT policy defined\n  - Example: If a policy "allows anyone to submit", add one so "submitters can view their own submissions"\n- Frontend and backend permissions must be aligned\n  - No permission, no interaction\n  - All submit-capable forms must have explicit, role-based permissions\n- PostgREST silently returns 0 affected rows (no error) when UPDATE/DELETE does not match RLS — writes appear to succeed but nothing changed. Tables the frontend needs to mutate must have explicit UPDATE/DELETE policies defined\n- Clear role boundaries\n  - Admins must have full read/write access\n  - Roles must have complete and secure permissions defined for every possible interaction scenario\n- All internal checks must use `SECURITY DEFINER`\n\n### Implementation Notes\n\n- RLS should only depend on **static columns or secure functions**\n- **Policy self-loop**: A policy\'s USING clause must not query the same table it protects — use a `SECURITY DEFINER` helper function instead (it bypasses RLS when querying the table)\n- Use public views to expose read-only access to selected fields of high-privilege tables\n\n## Storage Buckets\n\n- Create for image/file uploads only\n- **CRITICAL**: NEVER store images/videos as Base64 in database\n- ALL image/video assets MUST be uploaded to Supabase Storage\n- When third-party APIs return image/video URLs, transfer to Storage in Edge Function\n- buckets must be created in migration SQL via `supabase_apply_migration` — **do not** create them dynamically inside Edge Functions\n- Frontend validation: 1MB limit, snake_case filenames\n\n\n## Edge Functions\n\n### When to Use\n\n- **MANDATORY for third-party API calls**: ALL external API integrations (payment, weather, maps, etc.) MUST be implemented through Edge Functions\n- **STRICTLY FORBIDDEN**: Direct third-party API calls from client-side code (fetch/axios in frontend components)\n- Server-side secrets and service-role operations\n- Sensitive payment logic requiring secure environment\n\n### Authoring\n\n- Create files under `supabase/functions/<function_name>/`\n- **CRITICAL**: Use `supabase_deploy_edge_function` to deploy after modifying or creating Edge Function files\n- Put cross-domain content in the `_shared/` directory\n- No URL imports — only npm and JSR\n- Do not add secrets unless explicitly required by API documentation\n- Handle CORS properly\n- `supabase.sql` forbidden in Edge Functions\n- `supabase.raw` forbidden in Edge Functions — use `.rpc()` for atomic operations\n- Response Content-Type must be chosen only from: `[\'application/json\', \'application/octet-stream\', \'text/event-stream\', \'multipart/form-data\']`\n- Make proper use of optimistic locking to ensure that subsequent settlement operations in the state flow are executed only once, even if called multiple times\n\n\n## Supabase Auth\n\n- Your knowledge may be outdated. **MUST** call `skill_action(skill="login")` to refresh with the latest information\n- Any form of third-party login (OAuth or SSO) must use the login skill as the knowledge basis\n\n## Supabase Realtime (low-frequency feature)\n\nWhen realtime capability is genuinely needed, read `references/realtime.md` — it covers server-side publication switches, per-stack client subscription patterns, and RN/weapp limitations.\n\n**Multi-identity scenarios**: Identity selection / role assignment logic **must NOT** be placed on the frontend — it **MUST** be encapsulated in an Edge Function.', observation=<ObservationType.SKILL: 'skill'>, skill='supabase-server', success=True, data={'skill_path':     18 // 调用 Edge Function 创建微信支付订单
    19 export async function createPaymentOrder(skuCode: string, quantity: number = 1): Promise<{ success: boolean; order?: Order; wechat_pay_url?: string; error?: string }> {
    20   try {
    21     const { data: { session } } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
    22     if (!session) {
    23       return { success: false, error: '请先登录' };
    24     }
    25 
    26     const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('create_payment_order', {
    27       body: { sku_code: skuCode, quantity },
    28     });
    29 
    30     if (error || !data?.success) {
    31       return { success: false, error: error?.message || data?.error || '创建订单失败' };
    32     }
    33 
    34     return {
    35       success: true,
    36       order: {
    37         id: data.order_id,
    38         order_no: data.order_no,
    39         user_id: session.user.id,
    40         status: 'pending',
    41         wechat_pay_url: data.wechat_pay_url,
    42         alipay_pay_url: null,
    43         pay_type: 'wechat',
    44         total_amount: data.total_amount,
    45         created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    46         updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    47       },
    48       wechat_pay_url: data.wechat_pay_url,
    49     };
    50   } catch (err: any) {
    51     return { success: false, error: err.message || '网络错误' };
    52   }
    53 }

const supabaseUrl = Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!;

const CORS = {
  'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
  'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'authorization, content-type',
};

// ── 语言检测 ──────────────────────────────────────────────
function detectLanguage(text: string): 'zh' | 'en' | 'mixed' {
  const total = text.length;
  if (total === 0) return 'zh';
  const zhChars = (text.match(/[\u4e00-\u9fff]/g) || []).length;
  const ratio = zhChars / total;
  if (ratio > 0.4) return 'zh';
  if (ratio < 0.1) return 'en';
  return 'mixed';
}

// ── 构建分析提示词 ─────────────────────────────────────────
function buildPrompt(
  subjectName: string,
  relationship: string,
  background: string,
  assets: string,
  lang: 'zh' | 'en' | 'mixed',
): string {
  const isZh = lang !== 'en';
  return isZh
    ? `你是「魔镜」——跨境家庭关系风险筛查 AI。请根据以下信息，输出结构化 JSON 风险评估报告。

调查对象：${subjectName}
关系类型：${relationship || '未指定'}
背景描述：${background || '无'}
资产/财务信息：${assets || '无'}

【风险等级判定规则】
- high（红灯-高风险）：满足任一即触发：有法院被执行人记录、有未结诉讼或刑事案件、企业被吊销/经营异常、身份完全无法验证、资产声明与公开信息严重矛盾、存在家暴/欺诈相关记录
- medium（黄灯-需关注）：满足任一但无高风险项：婚龄<1年且对方无公开信息、声明资产无法佐证、有过往已结诉讼、信息缺失超过3项、用户材料与公开信息存在差异
- low（绿灯-低风险）：身份可验证且信息基本吻合、无负面公开记录、资产声明有公开信息佐证
- unknown（白灯-信息不足）：所有公开渠道均无此人记录，或信息量不足以做出任何判断

【综合评级四档】
- "🔴 红灯 - 高风险" / "🟡 黄灯 - 需关注" / "🟢 绿灯 - 低风险" / "⚪ 白灯 - 信息不足"

请严格按以下 JSON 格式输出（不要有任何前缀文字，不要截断 JSON）：
{
  "identityVerification": {
    "name": "<对象姓名>",
    "age": "<根据背景推断的年龄区间，如 30-40，无法推断填 '未知'>",

      const { data: { user } } = await supabase.auth.getUser(authHeader.replace('Bearer ', ''));
      if (!user) {
        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: '用户未登录' }), {
          status: 401,
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...CORS },
        });
      }
    }

    // 拼接全部输入文本用于语言检测
    const fullText = [subjectName, relationship, background, assets].join(' ');
    const lang = detectLanguage(fullText);
    const prompt = buildPrompt(subjectName, relationship, background, assets, lang);

    console.log(`[magic_mirror] lang=${lang}, subject="${subjectName}"`);

    // ── 按语言路由并行调用 ──────────────────────────────
    const calls: Promise<{ label: string; data: Record<string, unknown> | null; ms: number }>[] = [];

    // 英文或混合 → 加入 Groq
    if (lang === 'en' || lang === 'mixed') {
      if (GROQ_API_KEY) {
        calls.push(callModel({
          baseUrl: 'https://api.groq.com/openai/v1',
          apiKey: GROQ_API_KEY,
          model: 'llama-3.3-70b-versatile',
          prompt,
          label: 'Groq-Llama3.3-70B',
        }));
      } else {
        console.warn('[magic_mirror] GROQ_API_KEY not configured, skipping Groq');
      }
    }

    // 中文、英文、混合 → 硅基流动 Qwen2.5-7B
    if (SILICONFLOW_API_KEY) {
      calls.push(callModel({
        baseUrl: 'https://api.siliconflow.cn/v1',
        apiKey: SILICONFLOW_API_KEY,
        model: 'Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct',
        prompt,
        label: 'SiliconFlow-Qwen2.5-7B',
      }));

      // 中文、英文、混合 → 硅基流动 DeepSeek-V3
      calls.push(callModel({
        baseUrl: 'https://api.siliconflow.cn/v1',
        apiKey: SILICONFLOW_API_KEY,
        model: 'deepseek-ai/DeepSeek-V3',
        prompt,
        label: 'SiliconFlow-DeepSeek-V3',
      }));
    } else {
      console.warn('[magic_mirror] SILICONFLOW_API_KEY not configured, skipping SiliconFlow');
    }

    if (calls.length === 0) {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'AI 服务密钥未配置，请联系管理员' }), {
        status: 503,
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...CORS },
      });
    }

    // 取最快成功的模型结果（Promise.any），超时 25s 兜底
    const raceWithTimeout = <T,>(promises: Promise<T>[], ms: number): Promise<T> =>
      Promise.any([
        ...promises,
        new Promise<T>((_, reject) => setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('timeout')), ms)),
      ]);

    let reportData;
    try {
      // 先等最快的一路返回
      const first = await raceWithTimeout(calls, 25000);
      reportData = synthesize([first], subjectName);
    } catch {
      // 如果 Promise.any 全部失败，尝试 allSettled 取任何成功的结果
      const settled = await Promise.allSettled(calls);
      const successes = settled
        .filter((r): r is PromiseFulfilledResult<Awaited<(typeof calls)[0]>> => r.status === 'fulfilled')
        .map((r) => r.value);
      if (successes.length === 0) throw new Error('所有 AI 模型均无响应，请稍后重试');
      reportData = synthesize(successes, subjectName);
    }

    console.log(`[magic_mirror] synthesized, modelsUsed=${(reportData._meta as Record<string, unknown>)?.modelsUsed}`);

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ reportData, lang }), {
      status: 200,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...CORS },
    });
  } catch (err: unknown) {
    const msg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
    console.error('[magic_mirror ERROR]', msg);
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: msg || '服务内部错误' }), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', ...CORS },
    });
  }
});
